      $svjq("#search12_68f76f00163d8f4d6eba334").svAutoComplete({
         source: "/2.68f76f00163d8f4d6eb9b22/12.68f76f00163d8f4d6eba334.xml?state=autoComplete",
         minLength: 2,
         delay: 200
      });
   // Fallback if browser doesn't support the html5 placeholder attribute
   if (!sv.ClientUtil.supportsPlaceholder) {
      // Ensure initial value
      if ($svjq("#search12_68f76f00163d8f4d6eba334").val() == "") {
         $svjq("#search12_68f76f00163d8f4d6eba334").val("Ange sökord");
      }
      // Ensures 'search here' text is properly cleared when entering search field
      $svjq("#search12_68f76f00163d8f4d6eba334").focusin(function() {
         if ($svjq("#search12_68f76f00163d8f4d6eba334").val() == "Ange sökord") {
            $svjq("#search12_68f76f00163d8f4d6eba334").val("");
            return false;
         }
      });
      // Ensures 'search here' text is properly set when leaving search field
      $svjq("#search12_68f76f00163d8f4d6eba334").focusout(function() {
         if ($svjq("#search12_68f76f00163d8f4d6eba334").val() == "") {
            $svjq("#search12_68f76f00163d8f4d6eba334").val("Ange sökord");
            return false;
         }
      });
   }
      // Submit, blocks empty search and 'search here' search
      $svjq("#search12_68f76f00163d8f4d6eba334button").click(function() {
         var qry = $svjq("#search12_68f76f00163d8f4d6eba334").val();
         if (qry == "") {
            $svjq("#search12_68f76f00163d8f4d6eba334").val("Ange sökord");
            return false;
         } else if (qry == "Ange sökord") {
            return false;
         }
      });
      // Invokes the search button if user presses the enter key (needed in IE)
      $svjq("#search12_68f76f00163d8f4d6eba334").keypress(function(e) {
         if (e.which == 13) {
            $svjq("#search12_68f76f00163d8f4d6eba334button").focus().click();
            return false;
         }
      });
   });
